role="main"><div class="layout-md-rail"><div class="layout-md-rail__primary"><div class="ad-slot hidden-print hidden-for-md hidden-for-lg"><div class="ad-slot__container" style="min-height:251px"><div id="ad-post-mpu-top-mobile" class="dfp-ad" data-adsizes="[[[970,250],[]],[[728,90],[]],[[0,0],[[300,251],[300,250],&quot;fluid&quot;]]]" data-adtargets="{&quot;pos&quot;:[&quot;mpu1&quot;,&quot;top&quot;,&quot;recipe_top&quot;]}" data-adrefresh="true"><div class="ad-slot__text body-copy-small pt-xs pb-xs chromatic-ignore">Advertisement</div></div></div></div><div class="post__content"><div class="mb-lg hidden-print"><div id="recipetools" class="whisk hidden-print"></div></div><div class="editor-content mb-lg hidden-print js-piano-preview-content" data-placement="Introduction"><div class="brightcove brightcove__player-container" data-gtm-class="video"><div class="chromatic-ignore brightcove__player vjs-playlist-player-container" data-testid="brightcove-player"></div></div></div><div class="js-piano-inline"></div><div class="editor-content mb-lg hidden-print js-piano-locked-content" data-placement="Introduction"></div><div class="mb-lg" data-placement="Body"><div class="row recipe__instructions"><section class="recipe__ingredients col-12 mt-md col-lg-6" data-component="IngredientsList" data-feature="Recipe Instructions"><h2 class="mb-md section-heading-1">Ingredients</h2><section><ul class="list"><li class="pb-xxs pt-xxs list-item list-item--separator">2 tsp <a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/cumin-glossary" data-component="Link">cumin seeds</a></li><li class="pb-xxs pt-xxs list-item list-item--separator">pinch <a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/chilli-glossary" data-component="Link">chilli flakes</a></li><li class="pb-xxs pt-xxs list-item list-item--separator">2 tbsp <a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/olive-oil-glossary" data-component="Link">olive oil</a></li><li class="pb-xxs pt-xxs list-item list-item--separator">600g <a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/carrots-glossary" data-component="Link">carrots,</a> washed and coarsely grated (no need to peel)</li><li class="pb-xxs pt-xxs list-item list-item--separator">140g <!-- -->split red lentils</li><li class="pb-xxs pt-xxs list-item list-item--separator">1l <!-- -->hot vegetable stock<!-- --> (from a cube is fine)</li><li class="pb-xxs pt-xxs list-item list-item--separator">125ml <a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/milk-glossary" data-component="Link">milk</a> (to make it dairy-free, see &#x27;try&#x27; below)</li><li class="pb-xxs pt-xxs list-item list-item--separator"><a class="link link--styled" href="/glossary/yogurt-glossary" data-component="Link">plain yogurt</a> and naan bread, to serve</li></ul></section></section><section class="recipe__method-steps mb-lg col-12 col-lg-6" data-placement="MethodList"><h3 class="mb-xs section-heading-1">Method</h3><div class="grouped-list"><ul class="grouped-list__list list"><li class="pb-xs pt-xs list-item"><span class="mb-xxs heading-6">STEP 1</span><div class="editor-content"><p>Heat a large <a href="https://www.bbcgoodfood.com/review/five-best-saucepans">saucepan</a> and dry-fry 2 tsp cumin seeds and a pinch of chilli flakes for 1 min, or until they start to jump around the pan and release their aromas.</p><div class="ad-placement" data-count="166"></div></div></li><li class="pb-xs pt-xs list-item"><span class="mb-xxs heading-6">STEP 2</span><div class="editor-content"><p>Scoop out about half with a spoon and set aside. Add 2 tbsp olive oil, 600g coarsely grated carrots, 140g split red lentils, 1l hot vegetable stock and 125ml milk to the pan and bring to the boil.</p><div class="ad-placement" data-count="368"></div></div></li><li class="pb-xs pt-xs list-item"><span class="mb-xxs heading-6">STEP 3</span><div class="editor-content"><p>Simmer for 15 mins until the lentils have swollen and softened.</p><div class="ad-placement" data-count="437"></div></div></li><li class="pb-xs pt-xs list-item"><span class="mb-xxs heading-6">STEP 4</span><div class="editor-content"><p>Whizz the soup with a <a href="https://www.bbcgoodfood.com/content/top-five-hand-blenders">stick blender</a> or in a <a href="https://www.bbcgoodfood.com/review/best-food-processors">food processor</a> until smooth (or leave it chunky if you prefer).</p><div class="ad-placement" data-count="550"></div></div></li><li class="pb-xs pt-xs list-item"><span class="mb-xxs heading-6">STEP 5</span><div class="editor-content"><p>Season to taste and finish with a dollop of plain yogurt and a sprinkling of the reserved toasted spices. Serve with warmed naan breads.</p></div></li></ul></div></section></div></div><div class="post__content-end row hidden-print"><div class="col-12"><div class="editor-content mb-lg" data-placement="Summary"><h6 id="recipe-tips-8a92a7fa">RECIPE TIPS</h6><section class="highlight-box" data-feature="Highlight Box" data-feature-variant="editorial"><div class="highlight-box__content editor-content"><h6>USE A SOUP MAKER</h6><p>Save time and effort by placing all your ingredients in a soup maker and whizzing up a delicious soup in no time. Read our review on some of the <a href="https://www.bbcgoodfood.com/review/best-soup-makers-test">best soup makers</a> available.</div></section><section class="highlight-box" data-feature="Highlight Box" data-feature-variant="editorial"><div class="highlight-box__content editor-content"><h6>IF YOU WANT TO USE A SLOW COOKER...</h6><p>Place half the cumin seeds, half the chilli flakes, the oil, carrots, lentils and 700ml stock into your slow cooker pot. Cover and cook on High for 3 hours until the lentils are tender. Dry-fry the remaining cumin seeds and chilli flakes just until fragrant. When the lentils are done, stir in the milk and whizz up the soup depending on how chunky you\'d like it.</div></section><section class="highlight-box" data-feature="Highlight Box" data-feature-variant="editorial"><div class="highlight-box__content editor-content"><h6>MAKE IT MOROCCAN</h6><p>Substitute the chilli flakes and cumin seeds for a few teaspoons of harissa paste. You could add cooked shredded chicken at the end of cooking, too.</div></section><section class="highlight-box" data-feature="Highlight Box" data-feature-variant="editorial"><div class="highlight-box__content editor-content"><h6>MAKE IT DAIRY-FREE</h6><p>For a richer but dairy-free alternative, use a can of reduced-fat coconut milk instead of the milk.</div></section></div></div></div><p class="post__publication-link hidden-print">Recipe from Good Food magazine, <!-- -->October 2005</p></div><div class="pt-sm pb-sm full-width"><section class="hidden-print"><div class="dynamic-cards-list pr-sm pl-sm pt-md pb-md" style="background-color:rgba(240, 240, 240, 1)" data-feature="GoesWellWith" data-placement="recipeBelowEndSummary"><h3 class="mb-lg text-center heading-3">Goes well with</h3></div></section></div><div class="pocket hidden-print mb-md" data-placement="recipeBelowContent"><div class="mt-md"></div></div><div
